### 2. 郊区后院里困惑外星人的微缩立体模型

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，旨在创建一个纪录片风格的微缩世界立体模型。场景设定在一个郊区后院，一个微小的外星人正在滑稽地误用地球上的日常物品，例如牵着吸尘器散步，并试图种植电视遥控器。该提示详细说明了复杂的物理细节、灯光、构图，甚至要求加入一个正在场景中工作的逼真人造工匠，并使用上传的图像来精确识别工匠的面部。

![郊区后院里困惑外星人的微缩立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966044376_kieu39_G-Dy-7ra0AAVHGE.jpg)

```
Professional photography, medium-wide shot. A massive, realistic diorama world filling the entire workspace horizon, depicting a cross-section of a suburban backyard where a confused alien is hilariously misusing everyday Earth objects. The structure features a typical wooden fence and garden shed merged with a UFO partially hidden behind bushes (with soft LED underglow). Intricate details include a miniature green alien figurine wearing a flower pot as a hat, attempting to "walk" a vacuum cleaner on a leash like a dog, using a garden hose as a telephone, sitting in a birdbath fully clothed reading a pizza menu upside-down, and trying to plant TV remote controls in soil like seeds. A confused golden retriever figurine watches with head tilted. On the patio, miniature human figures peek through window curtains looking shocked and bewildered. The lawn features misplaced items: umbrella stuck in ground upside-down filled with cereal, lawn chair hanging from tree branch, sprinkler shooting water straight up. The background consists entirely of physical 3D forms, featuring sculpted foam neighboring houses with lights on, clay trees, and a painted evening sky with tiny stars, with absolutely no flat backdrops. A realistic human artisan is positioned in the back-right background, actively working on the scene, using fine tweezers to adjust the tiny vacuum cleaner "leash," grinning widely at the absurdity. Dual-layer workspace lighting combines with warm evening suburban lighting plus soft UFO glow (blue-green LED) to highlight the contrast between normal suburban textures and surreal alien confusion. Compose the scene for a 9:16 vertical aspect ratio with balanced framing and no cropped elements. Ensure all primary subjects, key actions, and facial features remain within a central safe zone, avoiding edge cropping across the selected aspect ratio. If a human creator or artisan is present in the scene, render the person as a realistic individual. Use the uploaded image reference as the exact facial identity of the creator. Maintain consistent facial structure, proportions, and likeness. Do not reinterpret, stylize, or substitute the face.
```

[[Humorous Concept]]

### 6. 真实的真人秀节目广播截图 (2x2 网格)

**Author**: [TechHalla](https://x.com/techhalla)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂且结构化的提示，旨在生成一个 2x2 的图像网格，模仿原始、未经修饰的电视广播片段，特别是像《老大哥》这类真人秀节目的风格。它要求在屏幕上显示图形（时间戳、摄像机 ID），并为四个不同场景设定特定的视觉美学：家庭摩擦、忏悔室、夜视秘密和爆炸。

![真实的真人秀节目广播截图 (2x2 网格)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966010458_blfvy6_G-DrF0pW0AAFfQa.jpg)

```
**CORE INSTRUCTION FOR THE MODEL:**
Analyze the personality traits and potential conflicts of the CHARACTERS previously provided as input. You must infer how these specific individuals would interact and place them into the four scenarios below based on their likelihood to be involved in that specific type of scene (e.g., put gossips in the confessional, aggressors in the fight scene).

**MANDATORY VISUAL AESTHETIC ("Real Broadcast Look"):**
The images must NOT look like staged photography. They must look like raw, unpolished TV broadcast footage.
* **Crucial Details:** Every panel must include on-screen graphics: timestamps (e.g., "DAY 12 | 14:32"), camera location identifiers (e.g., "CAM 1 - LIVING AREA"), and a small, semi-transparent channel logo in a corner.
* **Textures:** Expect video grain, slight lens distortion, harsh fluorescent lighting, and occasional digital compression artifacts.

**GRID BREAKDOWN (2x2 Layout):**

**[TOP ROW]**
* **[PANEL 1: Top-Left] Domestic Friction (Kitchen/Living Area).** Wide-angle fixed CCTV camera shot. Harsh, unflattering overhead lighting. Based on inputs, show a tense moment of daily life—two characters with incompatible habits arguing over cleaning or food, while others sit uncomfortably in the background. The composition is messy and naturalistic.
* **[PANEL 2: Top-Right] The Confessional Booth (El Confesionario).** Tight, claustrophobic fish-eye lens close-up. The background is a simple, soundproofed wall. Select the character most likely to vent or gossip from the inputs. They are looking directly into the lens, highly emotional (crying or angrily gesturing), breaking the fourth wall.

**[BOTTOM ROW]**
* **[PANEL 3: Bottom-Left] Night Vision Secrets (Bedroom).** Monochrome green or grey infrared night-vision shot. Grainy, low fidelity. Total darkness in the room. Show two characters (strategic allies based on inputs) whispering conspiratorially in a bed, barely visible under covers.
* **[PANEL 4: Bottom-Right] The Explosion (Garden/Smoking Area).** Chaotic, slightly shaky "handheld camera" feel, as if an operator ran to catch the action. High drama. A screaming argument at a party or nighttime gathering. The most volatile characters from the inputs are being physically separated by others. Flashing lights or dramatic shadows.

**STYLE:** Raw reality TV broadcast screenshots, 2x2 grid, highly detailed, 4k
```

[[Reality TV Broadcast Screenshot 2x2 Grid]]

```
{

    "type": "3D stylized female character",
    "age_range": "Young adult / Teen",

      "hair": "Shoulder-length, straight, dark brown, center-parted",
      "eyes": "Closed, smiling curve",
      "eyewear": "Round-framed glasses, soft pink/mauve color"
    },
    "pose": "Sitting, waving one hand, one hand resting on lap"
  },

    "top": "Oversized light grey sweatshirt with a minimalist line-art graphic of a rabbit holding a blue umbrella",
    "bottom": "White shorts or trousers"
  },

    "category": "3D Illustration / Digital Art",

    "lighting": "Soft, diffused studio lighting, high-key",
    "texture": "Smooth matte skin, soft fabric texture on the sweatshirt",
    "color_palette": "Pastel tones, neutrals, soft pinks, and greys"
  },
  "composition": {
    "framing": "Medium shot, waist-up",
    "background": "Solid off-white, clean, minimalist",
    "viewpoint": "Eye level"
  },

    "octane render",
```

### 12. 梵高博物馆自拍提示词

**Author**: [Keskin](https://x.com/craftian_keskin)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张文森特·梵高在安静的艺术博物馆内，用智能手机自拍的逼真、抓拍照片。该提示要求 AI 使用一张上传的图片作为梵高自画像的参考，该自画像必须在他身后的画框中可见，同时强调现代手机相机美学（广角镜头、胶片颗粒、逼真的反光）与 19 世纪服饰的结合。

![梵高博物馆自拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966118793_w9gpy3_G9_NxoYXUAA4n9v.jpg)
![梵高博物馆自拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966119529_de0slb_G9_NxobWYAAZEkK.jpg)

```
Model-ready prompt (use your uploaded image as reference for the framed painting):
A candid smartphone selfie photo taken inside a quiet art museum gallery. Vincent van Gogh stands in the foreground at arm’s length holding a modern phone toward the camera, smiling warmly with bright eyes. He is positioned so that, right beside him on the wall, there’s a framed display of his own famous self-portrait (match the look/colors/brushwork of the reference image), clearly visible and recognizable behind glass. The museum setting includes a clean white wall, subtle placard label near the frame, soft ambient gallery lighting, and gentle reflections on the frame’s protective glass.
 Composition: vertical selfie framing, slightly wide-angle, his face close to lens, the framed painting fully in shot over his shoulder; natural perspective distortion typical of phone selfies.
 Wardrobe/appearance: 19th-century attire (simple jacket/coat), short reddish beard, neatly combed hair; expression friendly and proud.
 Lighting: soft diffused museum track lights, even exposure, mild highlight on face, realistic shadow falloff.
 Style: photorealistic modern phone photo with film grain, slight halation, subtle color noise, gentle vignette; crisp but not overly sharp, authentic candid moment.
 Camera cues: iPhone-like wide lens (≈24–26mm equivalent), f/1.8 look, shallow-to-moderate depth of field, slight motion micro-blur, realistic skin texture, accurate museum reflections.
Optional negative prompt:
painting/illustration look, heavy stylization, cartoon, warped face, extra fingers, deformed hands, duplicated phone, text artifacts, unreadable signage, watermark, logo, over-sharpening, HDR haloing, extreme blur, low-res, uncanny eyes, incorrect museum context
ar 3:4
```

### 13. 融入角色的御神签（求签）生成提示

**Author**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: ja

> 一个给 Nano Banana Pro 的详细提示，用于生成一张逼真的快照照片：一只手拿着一张从日本神社的机器中取出的御神签（求签纸）。该提示将一个参考角色融入机器的海报和求签纸的设计中，强调真实感、纹理、光线，并根据角色的个性幽默地定制签文内容。

![融入角色的御神签（求签）生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966166203_6ofqdu_G-DJISja0AAI9Hg.jpg)
![融入角色的御神签（求签）生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966167240_alukrt_G-DJIXBbEAABa-k.jpg)
![融入角色的御神签（求签）生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966167882_zfbwj5_G-DJI7baYAAOhCE.jpg)
![融入角色的御神签（求签）生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966168582_wszszu_G-DJJL9bwAAx-w2.jpg)

```
日本の神社の境内に設置された「おみくじ販売機」から出てきた
おみくじを、人物の手が一枚だけ持ち上げている実写スナップ写真。

構図：
・やや斜め上からの自然なスナップ写真構図。
・手前におみくじが画面に大きく写し出され、背景にはおみくじ機本体が映り込んでいる。
・おみくじ機にはポスターがあり、参考画像のキャラクターが表示されている。
・背景には初詣らしい神社の雰囲気（鳥居、木材、注連縄、正月飾り）を参考画像の世界観に寄せて少しアレンジする。新年の装いの人々も映り込んでいる。
おみくじ機のポスターとおみくじの挿絵に使用するキャラクターは参考画像を完璧に模倣する。

◆ キャラクター名
・指定がない場合は、参考画像の外見・雰囲気・色味・性格を読み取り、
強烈なユーモアを込めた和風寄りのキャラクター名を自動生成する。

◆ おみくじ紙（質感）
・和紙のような繊維感があり、折りたたまれていた跡がくっきり残っている。
・少しだけシワがあり、本物感のある質感。
・各エリアは参考キャラクターの特徴を反映した
和モダンでスタイリッシュなフレームで区切られている。
・手に持つ指と紙の影が自然に落ち、光源の方向が明確。

◆ おみくじタイトル（参考画像から生成）
・参考画像キャラの性格・色・世界観からタイトルを生成。
・紙の最上部に大きく印字。
・フォントは和風ロゴ調だが、色味は参考画像のトーンに合わせる。

・参考画像キャラクターのイラストやアイコンを、
おみくじ紙の2〜3箇所に小さく配置。

◆ おみくじ内容（通常形式）
・今年の運勢({argument name="運勢" default="大吉～大凶"}から※※必ずランダムで選ぶ※※その上で、参考画像の雰囲気に合わせてめちゃくちゃにアレンジする) ＋ 5〜6項目を日本語で印字。
・各項目には運勢表記と、
約30文字程度の一言コメントを添える。
・文章は本物のおみくじ調で、
参考キャラクターの特徴をユーモラスに誇張した内容にする。
・項目名は参考画像のキャラクター性から自由にアレンジする。
・特徴的な項目いくつかに、参考画像のキャラクターの適した場面の挿絵を入れる

◆ おみくじ機（背景）
大きな画像が表示されている。画像には
・参考画像のキャラクターを新年らしい装いにアレンジして表示
・おみくじ名を大きく表示
・参考画像から読み取った特徴を自由な発想で飛躍させた売り文句等
テキストとキャラクターを豊富に表示する。フォントデザインは参考画像の雰囲気に合わせる。
```

[[Omikuji Fortune Slip With Character Design]]

### 18. 东京超写实夜间智能手机抓拍照片

**Author**: [zayan](https://x.com/HustleXR)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、超现实的图像生成提示，旨在模仿在东京人行道上夜间拍摄的原始、不完美、真实的手机抓拍照片。它指定了刺眼的闪光灯照明、严重的运动模糊，以及主体对相机做出自发反应，强调一种未经修饰、噪点多的美学。

![东京超写实夜间智能手机抓拍照片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966004785_u9e22x_G-C_Gkoa8AAr2Zk.jpg)

```
Ultra-realistic candid smartphone photograph,
9:16 vertical.

Use the attached image only as a strong visual inspiration for general facial proportions and vibe,
while ensuring the generated subject remains fully original, non-identifiable, and not a face copy.

Scene
Nighttime on a quiet Tokyo city sidewalk beside a building with white ceramic tile walls.
The subject is walking past the camera, partially side-on, captured mid-step in a rushed, accidental moment.

Poses & Gestures (combined naturally)
The subject reacts instinctively to being photographed:
turning her head back mid-walk as if surprised,
raising one hand close to the lens to partially block the camera,
shy, restrained smile forming as she suppresses laughter,
body angled in half-profile while continuing to walk forward,
motion carries her slightly out of frame, imperfect framing.
Expressions are subtle and spontaneous — embarrassed, playful, fleeting — never posed.

Camera & Motion
Shot on a modern smartphone, handheld, rushed capture. Strong uncontrolled camera shake. Heavy directional motion blur across the raised hand, hair, and face. Facial features appear smeared and streaked by movement, faintly recognizable but distorted. Partial ghosting around the body. Imperfect framing, subject nearly leaving the frame.

Lighting
Flash-only lighting fired mid-motion. Harsh flash highlights on skin and hand. Deep surrounding darkness. Uneven exposure, blown highlights, hard shadows typical of hurried night phone photography.

Background
White ceramic tile wall stretches into streaked light bands due to motion blur. Street surroundings fade into darkness with minimal readable detail.

Mood
Candid, shy, slightly playful. Feels intrusive, raw, imperfect, and authentic — like a fleeting memory accidentally captured and never meant to be perfect.

Image Quality
Extremely noisy. Heavily blurred. Raw smartphone look. Not cinematic. Not editorial. Not polished.

Negative Prompt
anime, illustration, painting, stylized,
studio lighting, beauty lighting, soft portrait,
sharp focus, clean face, perfect anatomy, smooth skin,
fashion editorial, posed portrait, cinematic grading, film still,
tripod shot, professional photography,
identity match, face copy, real person replication.

– no anime, illustration, cartoon, or doll-like features
– no beauty filters, no airbrushed skin
– no face reshaping or eye enlargement
– no exaggerated body curves
– no extra or missing fingers
– no distorted arms, shoulders, or neck
– no studio or cinematic lighting
– no fashion posing
```

### 31. 超浅景深街头抓拍人像，写实风格

**Author**: [Anissa](https://x.com/SimplyAnnisa)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超现实、抓拍的街头时尚肖像。核心目的是实现极浅的景深，使中景中的单一主体保持锐利，同时将移动的人群和城市背景渲染成柔和的模糊/散景效果。它详细说明了构图、光线（电影般的柔和对比）以及关键的相机光学特性（长焦镜头、大光圈）。

![超浅景深街头抓拍人像，写实风格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966174010_ytlmug_G-CV_FEa0AAmStF.jpg)

```
Core Intent: Create a photorealistic candid street-fashion portrait with extreme shallow depth of field where a single woman is sharply in focus in the mid-ground, surrounded by a moving crowd rendered as soft blur/bokeh. Preserve the exact framing, subject placement, color grade, and atmosphere.

1) Composition & Framing (LOCK)

•Aspect: 4:5 vertical.

•Camera height: chest-to-eye level (slightly above the subject’s shoulder line).

•Framing: mid-ground subject centered slightly left-of-center, from upper chest to top of head clearly visible; shoulders included; background heavily blurred.

•Foreground: two large blurred human shapes frame the subject:

•Left foreground: blurred middle-aged man occupying left third, grey/blue jacket, face out of focus.

•Right foreground: blurred person occupying right-lower quadrant (dark hair), also out of focus.

•Mid-right: blurred older bald man head/shoulder visible behind subject’s right shoulder.

•Background: dense city street with yellow taxi/cab shapes and warm orange bokeh lights; tall urban forms dissolve into creamy blur.

2) Subject (Primary)

•Person: young adult woman, fair/light skin, subtle freckles, natural editorial beauty.

•Hair: medium brown, messy low updo/bun with loose wisps; slightly damp/urban texture; flyaways framing face.

•Expression: calm, slightly serious/curious; lips relaxed; eyes looking directly toward camera with a soft, neutral intensity.

•Pose: body facing right (3/4 profile), head turned back over left shoulder to look at camera.

3) Wardrobe & Accessories (Exact Feel)

•Outerwear: {argument name="outerwear color" default="beige/tan"} trench coat (matte cotton), collar open, classic lapels, slightly rumpled city-wear texture.

•Bag: small shoulder bag with thin gold chain strap on her right shoulder; strap catches a bit of light; bag itself mostly hidden.

•Jewelry: small earring visible (subtle, warm tone).

4) Environment (Street Mood)

•Busy metropolitan sidewalk/street scene, crowd density high.

•Background palette: teal/green-grey city haze + yellow cab + warm orange bokeh lights.

•No readable signage, no sharp background details—everything behind subject remains creamy blur.

5) Lighting (LOCK)

•Natural daylight, overcast-to-soft sun (diffused), no harsh shadows.

•Subject face evenly lit with gentle highlights on cheekbones and nose; cinematic soft contrast.

6) Camera & Optics (CRITICAL)

•Look: telephoto candid portrait with strong compression.

•Lens: 85mm–135mm range, wide open (f/1.4–f/2.0).

•Focus: tack-sharp on subject’s eyes and eyelashes; foreground and background strongly out of focus.

•Depth: creamy bokeh, smooth falloff, mild cat-eye bokeh at edges.

•Shutter/feel: background crowd appears naturally blurred from DOF; slight motion blur suggested in foreground figures.

7) Color Science / Grade (LOCK)

•Cinematic teal/green wash in shadows and background.

•Warm highlights (skin tones natural, slightly warm).

•Yellow taxi pops softly; orange bokeh lights glow.

•Fine
```

[[Candid Urban Photography]]

### 34. 足球商业广告片场的电影级摄影棚拍摄

**Author**: [Guillermo Castellanos](https://x.com/guicastellanos1)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个宽幅电影镜头，描绘一个专业的电影拍摄现场，专门为一个足球商业广告而设。场景设置在“The Volume”内，巨大的弧形 LED 墙上显示着动感的足球氛围，一架 Arri Alexa 摄影机安装在轨道车上，还有工作人员，强调体积光和变形镜头特性。

### 36. 2000 年代小型数码相机纹理提示

**Author**: [ぴょんきち|AI兄さん](https://x.com/yarakashiyama_)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: ja

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供一个详细的提示，用于将 2000 年代卡片数码相机（如佳能 EOS Kiss 系列）的纹理和美学应用于上传的照片。目标是克服 AI 图像的“不自然完美”，通过特定的光照（黄金时段，左上方强烈的定向光）、色彩分级（暖色调，柔和色）和纹理（细微的胶片颗粒）实现真实、富有情感和电影感的画面。

![2000 年代小型数码相机纹理提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966166379_td6tml_G-B1sLsXcAAfU1d.jpg)
![2000 年代小型数码相机纹理提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966167787_1adxqi_G-B1syCXIAA6-ow.jpg)

```
アップロードされた写真に、2000年代初頭のコンパクトデジタルカメラ（コンデジ）特有の質感を再現してください。元の被写体、ポーズ、背景、構図はすべてそのまま維持すること。全体の雰囲気は静かで親密、かつ映画のような情緒を感じる仕上がりに。柔らかなメランコリーと、ファッション誌のようなナチュラルな美しさを融合させます。

光はゴールデンアワーの自然光。左上から強い指向性のある光を当て、顔や胸元にドラマチックな影を落としてください。明部と柔らかな影のコントラストを強めることで、夢心地でありながら現実味のある質感を高めます。照明は、健康的な輝きを持つ、暖かく明るい肌のトーンを強調するように。

穏やかなフィルム粒子（グレイン）を加え、レタッチは最小限に留めてレンダリングします。ハイライトを抑え、温かみのある白を基調とした、わずかにパステルがかったカラーグレーディングを施してください。肌は露出オーバーを避け、自然で明るい、優しいピーチトーンに。写真は、{argument name="カメラモデル" default="キヤノンEOS Kissシリーズ"}のような視覚的特徴を維持し、鮮明でありながらも柔らかなディテール、自然な質感、温かみのあるダイナミックレンジを強調してください。画像がぼやけている場合はアップスケールを実行すること。

厳守事項：顔と「被験者の髪の毛」。
```

[[Film Grain Texture]]

### 41. Q 版角色“吐舌眨眼”姿势生成提示词

**Author**: [Yukinobu Kurata : 倉田幸暢](https://x.com/YukinobuKurata)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的结构化提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro 生成一个摆出“Tehepero”姿势（眨眼并稍微伸出舌头）的 Q 版角色。它指定了面部表情、身体姿势、摄像机角度（高角度，24 毫米等效）和构图（全身、居中、简单白色背景）。此提示需要一个现有的角色图像作为输入。

![Q 版角色“吐舌眨眼”姿势生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804134113_e2884v_G-BBV6TbcAMmljl.jpg)

```
subject:
    description: "添付画像のちびキャラが、「テヘペロ」のポーズをしている"
    character_style:
      - "ちびキャラ"

  expression_and_pose:
    facial_expression:
      - "右目をウインクしている"
      - "舌は口の端から上向きに少し出ている（「てへぺろ」）"
    pose:
      - "右手の握りこぶしで、側頭部の真横の高い位置を、軽くコツンと叩く仕草をしている"
      - "左腕は下方向へまっすぐ伸ばしている"

  body_orientation:
    torso:
      - "体の正面がカメラに対して完全な正面ではなく、少し斜め（3/4気味）を向いている"

  gaze:
    direction: "カメラ目線"
    quality:
      - "やわらかい正面視線"
      - "見る人を見つめる"
      - "優しいアイコンタクト"

  camera_and_composition:
    angle:
      - "ハイアングル"
      - "上から見下ろすが、顔はしっかり見える"
    perspective:
      - "誇張した遠近感"
      - "強いフォアショートニング（手前が大きく、奥が小さく見える）"
    lens:
      focal_length_equivalent: "24mm相当"
      distance: "カメラは被写体に近い"
    framing:
      - "全身が入る"
      - "中央配置"
    background:
      - "シンプルな白背景"
```

**Author**: [Yukinobu Kurata : 倉田幸暢](https://x.com/YukinobuKurata)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: ja

```
添付画像のちびキャラが、テヘペロのポーズをしている様子。
彼女は、片手をグーにして、その手をこめかみの位置に当てている。
彼女の舌は、彼女の口の端から、上向きに出ている。
彼女は、片目をウインクしている。

Camera angle: high angle (not overhead), looking down at the subject, face visible
Perspective: exaggerated perspective, strong foreshortening
Lens: wide-angle (24mm), close to camera
Composition: full body, centered, simple white background
Proportions: big head, small body (super-deformed)
```

### 64. Nano Banana Pro 专业图像编辑超级提示词

**Author**: [Alexander Inspira IA](https://x.com/Alex_Inspira)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: en

> 这是一个专为 Nano Banana Pro 环境中的专业图像编辑而设计的“超级提示词”。此提示词旨在直接复制和粘贴，以便对任何图像应用高级编辑指令。

![Nano Banana Pro 专业图像编辑超级提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767803998995_qh4iuu_G9_g6OKXoAEzg_I.jpg)

```
Eres un experto editor de imágenes profesional. Tu tarea es editar la imagen que te proporcionaré a continuación. Debes realizar las siguientes acciones:

1. **Análisis Inicial:** Evalúa la imagen en términos de composición, iluminación, colorimetría, nitidez y posibles imperfecciones.
2. **Corrección de Color y Tono:** Ajusta el balance de blancos, la exposición y el contraste para lograr un aspecto natural y vibrante. Mejora la saturación de manera sutil si es necesario.
3. **Retoque y Limpieza (si aplica):** Elimina cualquier elemento distractor, manchas o ruido digital. Si es un retrato, suaviza ligeramente la piel manteniendo la textura natural.
4. **Mejora de Nitidez:** Aplica un enfoque selectivo para resaltar los detalles clave sin introducir artefactos.
5. **Estilización (Opcional):** Si la imagen lo requiere, aplica un estilo sutil (ej. cinematográfico, vintage, alto contraste) que mejore la narrativa visual sin sobreprocesar.
6. **Formato de Salida:** Proporciona la imagen editada con la máxima calidad posible y una breve descripción de los cambios realizados.

**Instrucciones Adicionales:**
* Prioriza la naturalidad y la calidad profesional. Evita los efectos exagerados.
* Si la imagen es un retrato, asegúrate de que los ojos estén nítidos y brillantes.
* Si la imagen es un paisaje, potencia la profundidad y el cielo.

**Imagen a editar:** {argument name="Imagen a editar" default="[Inserta aquí la imagen]"}
```

[[Professional Image Editing Super Prompt]]

### 69. 原始高清打印肖像美学提示

**Author**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，旨在模拟一张原始、高清的实体打印肖像照片，捕捉纸张和墨水的纹理。它非常注重真实感、特定的光照（刺眼的影棚闪光灯），并包含创意文本叠加，非常适合生成年鉴或复古杂志档案美学。

![原始高清打印肖像美学提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804090631_kam4gr_G9_T8DWXkAAKLZF.jpg)

```
(3:4). A raw, high-definition photograph of a physical printed portrait taken with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. Everything is SHARP and in focus, capturing the physical textural reality of the paper grain and the ink-on-page in high resolution.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics as captured through high-end printed ink: visible micro-pores, natural "satin-finish" glow muted by paper texture, and fine peach fuzz along the jawline.
Expression: A perfectly aligned, symmetrical head-and-shoulders yearbook-style pose. Neutral but confident expression with a magnetic, "main character" gaze looking directly into the lens.
Silhouette Calibration: Despite the formal school tailoring, amplify the dominant structural bust volume and the aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist. Ensure the fit of the uniform highlights a high-impact, fit physique.
Outfit & Material Realism:

Clothing: A dark navy blue structured blazer with white piping, a crisp white collared shirt, and a dark navy striped silk tie.
Tension: The blazer and shirt show extreme material tension and a vacuum-tight fit, creating realistic physical interaction and "tension lines" that highlight her fit, symmetrical upper silhouette and anatomical depth.
The Printed Aesthetic (Hardware Emulation):

Surface Texture: The image features an authentic semi-gloss paper sheen with thin, realistic diagonal lamination glares reflecting off the ink surface across the cheeks and chest.
Ink Physics: Visible ink-absorption softening at the edges (not digital blur), fine paper grain texture, and a gentle warm undertone typical of vintage magazine archives. It looks like a scanned physical object.
Lighting & Composition:

Lighting: Direct frontal harsh studio flash (ID style). Even exposure with bright, sharp eye catchlights and minimal shadows, creating a flat but clean professional portrait look.
Background (SHARP): A flat, textured cool-blue studio backdrop, showing realistic ink-on-paper depth.
Creative "Pinterest" Text Overlay:

Center-aligned below the portrait in an ink-printed bold serif font: "{argument name="main text" default="MOST LIKELY TO..."}"
Below in smaller, elegant italic subtext: "{argument name="subtext" default="“Be the reason you check your phone every 5 minutes.”"}"
The text features slightly imperfect ink bleeding and natural letter-spacing, mimicking an authentic high-end physical printing process.
Quality: Raw scan/photo-of-print aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible paper fiber and digital ISO noise in the shadows, 8k resolution, looks physically touchable.
```

### 70. 穿着红色爱心毛衣的男士阅读特写

**Author**: [Zar⭕on](https://x.com/Zar_xplorer)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张亲密的、生活方式时尚的男性肖像编辑照片，描绘他坐在室内阅读的场景。重点在于实现超真实的皮肤纹理（可见毛孔、自然的色调变化）、柔和的自然窗户光线，以及带有心形图案的舒适红色针织毛衣的细节材质真实感。

![穿着红色爱心毛衣的男士阅读特写](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804099373_lul9b2_G9_TzdDbcAEvktF.jpg)

```
Concept & Mood

Intimate lifestyle–fashion editorial with quiet masculine warmth and thoughtful calm.
Soft, cozy atmosphere reminiscent of a private winter afternoon spent reading indoors.
Emotional restraint with gentle confidence — reflective, composed, subtly romantic without performance.
Feels like a real, candid moment captured naturally, not posed or styled for effect.

---

Subject & Anatomy

Adult man with realistic proportions and natural build.
Relaxed posture with subtle asymmetry — body leaning forward slightly, one arm resting on the table, head supported by the hand.
Natural weight distribution through the elbow and forearm resting on the surface.
No tension in the shoulders or neck, posture feels unforced and comfortable.

---

Pose & Perspective

Seated at a wooden table indoors.
Head gently tilted, cheek resting against the palm of the hand.
Other arm relaxed and folded near an open book on the table.
Camera positioned at eye level, slightly off-center, creating an intimate, conversational perspective.
Framing is mid-close portrait, focusing on face, hands, and upper torso.

---

Face & Expression

Soft, calm expression with a subtle, knowing half-smile.
Eyes relaxed and warm, making gentle eye contact with the camera.
Brows natural and expressive, conveying ease and quiet confidence rather than performance.
Facial hair neatly groomed with realistic density and texture.

---

Skin (Key Focus)

Highly realistic skin texture featuring:

visible pores

natural tonal variation

subtle under-eye texture

realistic beard shadow and transitions
Skin appears alive and tactile.
No smoothing, no beauty retouching, no artificial glow or plastic finish.

---

Hair & Grooming

Medium-length dark hair with natural volume and movement.
Softly tousled with slight wave, imperfect strands falling naturally across the forehead.
Hair density realistic, not styled or over-defined.
Beard neatly trimmed, edges soft and organic, not sharply sculpted.

---

Wardrobe & Styling

Cozy {argument name="sweater color" default="red"} knit sweater with small {argument name="motif" default="white heart"} motifs.
Fabric appears thick and warm, with:

visible knit texture

realistic folds and stretch around elbows and shoulders

natural drape and compression at contact points
Sweater reads as casual, intimate, and personal — not fashion-staged.

---

Environment & Props

Simple indoor setting with a wooden table surface.
An open book placed naturally in front of the subject, pages slightly curved and imperfect.
Background softly blurred, suggesting a quiet home or café interior.
No distracting elements, environment supports calm and intimacy.

---

Lighting

Soft natural window light only.
Light falls gently across the face, creating smooth highlight-to-shadow transitions.
Warm, diffused illumination with no harsh shadows.
No artificial lighting, no flash, no studio feel.

---

Camera & Optics

Photographer mindset.
Full-frame look with a 50–55mm perspective.
```

[[Visible Pore Skin Texture]]

### 74. 《鬼灭之刃》中我妻善逸的超写实跨界图像

**Author**: [F、Lai](https://x.com/Flai6666)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: zh

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细、超现实提示，用于生成动漫《鬼灭之刃》中的我妻善逸从一本巨大的实体漫画书中走出来的图像，将 8K 超逼真世界与黑白漫画风格融为一体。

![《鬼灭之刃》中我妻善逸的超写实跨界图像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804115206_v8i4fj_G9_MHmObcAA8Bsg.jpg)

```
一张令人惊叹的超写实8K照片，捕捉到了《{argument name="漫画名" default="鬼灭之刃"}》中的{argument name="人物名" default="我妻善逸"}（Zenitsu Agatsuma）正从一本巨大的实体漫画书中跨步走出的瞬间。

现实世界中的善逸：
善逸的形象是照片级真实的，头发是乱蓬蓬的金色和橙色，穿着质感真实的鬼杀队制服和他标志性的带有白色三角形图案的黄色羽织。他的表情坚定，眼神锐利，充满了决心，手中紧紧抓着带着刀鞘的日轮刀。他的身体一半已经踏在木质卧室地板上，另一半还在漫画书页中。
巨大的漫画书与互动：
一本巨大的、厚重的日文版《鬼灭之刃》漫画书摊开在略显磨损的木地板上。善逸打破了纸张的界限，纸页在他跨出的地方剧烈撕裂、卷曲和爆裂，纸屑和墨粉在空气中飞舞。

漫画页面内的细节（画中画）：
书页上呈现的是极其正宗的黑白日漫风格。
风格： 粗糙的黑色墨线、丰富的网点纸（screentone）纹理用于阴影、夸张的速度线。

布局： 严格的日式从右到左阅读顺序，是一个超现实的四格漫画（yonkoma）跨页。
内容： 在被打破的格子内部，可以看到一个被困住的、漫画画风的善逸。他穿着同样的衣服，在格子里流着面条泪，惊慌失措地敲打着漫画格子的边框，旁边配有巨大的日文拟声词，如「出られない！」（出不去！）、「えええ！？」和「ドンドンドン」（敲击声）。漫画中的他正惊恐地看着现实中的自己撕裂画面。

环境与光线：
卧室背景是柔焦的，有床脚、书架等生活气息的物品。自然的午后光线从侧面窗户射入，照亮了撕裂的纸张边缘和善逸衣服上的织物纹理，强调了现实与二维世界的强烈对比。
```

[[Demon Slayer Zenitsu Crossover From Manga]]

### 92. 逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示

**Author**: [小洲洲的AI日常](https://x.com/LZhou15365)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: zh

> 这是两步提示序列的第二部分，它将之前生成的逼真室内图像作为参考。目标是将该逼真房间转换为一个高度精细、透明的微缩建筑模型或立体模型，类似于博物馆展品。该提示强调在保留精确布局和比例的同时，专注于高端工业设计美学、透明亚克力/玻璃外壳、逼真的微缩材料以及精致的内部/外部照明对比。

![逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804127851_7f2xnk_G9-YpF7boAEz7nC.jpg)
![逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804128173_wwjjfd_G9-YpF-a4AAoYbt.jpg)
![逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804128251_4zd9hp_G9-YpF5aQAEHyRQ.jpg)
![逼真的室内透明微缩透视模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804132045_jxbcv8_G9-YpF5aMAAVeJC.jpg)

```
基于上传的“现实室内空间”参考图，生成一座“透明迷你小屋展示模型”。

【核心展示概念】
- 将原本的真实室内空间转化为一座“微缩比例的透明建筑模型”
- 像博物馆中展示的建筑剖面模型
- 房屋被完整封装在透明亚克力 / 玻璃外壳中
- 室内结构与家具完全可见

【结构与布局（必须严格保留）】
- 严格继承参考图中的室内布局与比例
- 墙体位置、家具摆放、动线关系完全一致
- 房间被整体缩小为迷你比例（如 1:10 / 1:12）
- 这是比例缩放，不是重新设计

【透明外壳设计】
- 外部为高透明度亚克力或玻璃材质
- 边角圆润，厚度清晰可见
- 局部采用剖切 / 切角结构，方便观察内部
- 透明外壳不遮挡主要室内视线

【室内表现（微缩但真实）】
- 所有家具按比例缩小
- 材质依然真实：木纹、布艺、金属
- 保留现实生活感，而非玩具感
- 灯具、植物、摆件清晰可见

【灯光系统（重点）】
- 室内暖色微光灯（如模型灯）
- 外部中性或冷色展示灯
- 形成内暖外冷的高级展示对比
- 轻微发光但不刺眼

【展示环境】
- 放置在极简展台 / 博物馆展示台上
- 背景干净（浅灰 / 深灰 / 黑色）
- 有真实比例参照（如展台阴影）

【视觉风格】
- 超写实
- 高级工业设计感
- 像 Apple / Muji / 建筑事务所的展示作品
- 非玩具风，非卡通风

【摄影与构图】
- 专业产品摄影或建筑模型摄影
- 中近景构图，略微俯视
- 景深，背景虚化
- 清晰对焦在透明小屋本体

【技术要求】
- 超高清细节
- 高折射率真实玻璃表现
- 正确反射与透视
- 无人物、无文字、无水印

作为艺术装置展示，具有当代设计与收藏价值
治愈、精致、让人一眼停住的视觉效果
避免玩具质感，避免塑料感，强调建筑模型与工业设计质感
高透明度、清晰折射边缘、干净玻璃
室内灯光清晰可见，像微缩模型灯光系统
```

[[Transparent Miniature Architectural Model]]

```
Use the uploaded reference photo. Low-resolution smartphone close-up selfie taken with a broken front camera screen. The image shows strong natural motion blur concentrated on the woman’s face, hair, and the cat, caused by weak autofocus, slow shutter speed, and slight hand movement while lying down. Blur appears uneven and organic, with soft smearing rather than smooth artificial blur. Facial features are partially obscured but still recognizable, with eyes, nose, and mouth visible as softened shapes. A young woman lies intimately on a cream-colored leather sofa. A light brown cat with bright green eyes is lying on the woman’s chest, pressing its body close and nuzzling its face against the woman’s cheek and jaw, partially covering her face. The cat’s head and the woman’s face overlap closely, creating intimate contact. Both the woman’s face and the cat’s face are noticeably blurred together, with softened edges and slight motion smear from small movements and breathing. The woman’s long brown hair is loose and slightly messy, falling over her forehead and partially blending into the cat’s fur due to blur. Hair strands appear heavily softened but still natural, not melted or warped. The cat’s fur texture is mostly lost, appearing as soft blurred patches consistent with low resolution and motion. Overall sharpness is low, with inconsistent focus across the frame — some tiny areas accidentally a bit clearer while most of the face and the cat remain out of focus. Flat, noisy skin texture with visible ISO noise, chroma noise, mild color banding, and muddy shadows typical of a cheap phone camera. The woman looks toward the lens with a soft, relaxed, intimate expression, though details are softened by blur. She wears simple, light-colored casual clothing, with fabric texture mostly lost. Lighting comes only from indoor room lights at night, slightly too bright, with mild overexposed highlights that do not completely blow out facial structure. Perspective distortion from the front camera wide-angle lens creates subtle stretching near the edges. The composition is very tight, awkward, and unintentional, filling the frame with the woman’s face and the cat’s body and head. The image feels like a raw, accidental selfie straight from the phone gallery — imperfect, intimate, noisy, naturally blurred, completely unedited, with no beautification and no AI enhancement.  NEGATIVE WARNINGS (important): high resolution, sharp focus, DSLR, cinematic lighting, studio lighting, ultra-detail, clean skin texture, beauty filter, HDR, professional photo, sharp edges, smooth look, AI enhancement, overprocessing, perfect blur, depth-of-field bokeh. ar 9:16
```

**Author**: [brindley](https://x.com/brindleyai)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细且结构化的图像生成提示，可能适用于 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 这样的模型，侧重于极致的真实感、特定的解剖比例、光照和构图。该提示分为几个部分，涵盖了主体、姿势、环境、相机和光照，并强烈强调保留精确的身体比例和逼真的皮肤纹理。

### 123. 超写实新中式人像，搭配 Gobo 灯光

**Author**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: zh

> 一个详细、多层次的提示词，用于生成一张超写实的商业肖像，描绘一位身着红色旗袍的年轻东亚女性，强调新中式美学、复杂的 Gobo 照明，以及极致的纹理细节，如可见的毳毛和次表面散射。此提示词专为高端时尚摄影渲染设计。

![超写实新中式人像，搭配 Gobo 灯光](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804118451_lzkurc_G97SDVIWEAEWMzT.jpg)

```
1. 宏观风格与媒介
- 核心媒介: 高清商业人像摄影 (High-end Commercial Photography)
- 美学流派: 新中式美学 (New Chinese Style), 节日时尚大片

2. 主体与IP身份
- 核心主体: 年轻东亚女性侧颜特写 (Close-up profile of young Asian woman)
- IP/名人锁定: 穿着{argument name="服装" default="红色旗袍"} (Red Cheongsam), 佩戴珍珠项链与红色花卉耳环

3. 世界逻辑与物理
- 物理法则: 真实光学投影 (Real optical projection), 面部光影贴合面部起伏
- 空间构成: 人眼平视视角 (Eye-level), 极近距离接触

4. 数据与信息层
- 文本提取: 无文本
- 品牌与符号: {argument name="前景元素" default="红色剪纸艺术前景"} (Red paper-cut art foreground) - 包含仙鹤、蝴蝶与牡丹纹样

5. 材质与纹理
- 核心材质: 超写实皮肤质感 (Hyper-realistic skin), 哑光卡纸 (Matte cardstock), 温润珍珠
- 触感细节: 逆光下可见的面部绒毛 (Visible vellus hair backlit), 次表面散射效果 (Subsurface scattering)

6. 光影与氛围
- 光照模型: Gobo投影布光 (Gobo lighting/Projected shadows) - 复杂的镂空花纹光影投射在人物面部
- 整体氛围: 金色暖阳侧逆光 (Warm golden hour light), 高饱和度喜庆红调, 梦幻且清晰

7. 技术参数
- 镜头与渲染: 85mm-100mm 微距镜头 (Macro lens), 浅景深 (Shallow depth of field), 前景虚化 (Bokeh foreground)
- 构图指令: 框式构图 (Framed composition), --ar 3:4
```

### 127. 赛博工业外骨骼物体转换提示

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: en

> 一个系统指令提示，旨在将任何输入对象（例如运动鞋或头骨）重新构想为复杂的、高性能的赛博工业装配体。它规定了将其解构为分段的碳纤维面板、带有发光工业电缆的内部机械装置以及精细的细节装饰，并以具有特定工作室照明和 Octane Bloom 效果的逼真 3D 产品照片形式呈现。

![赛博工业外骨骼物体转换提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682161991_14se7x_G9tjMDjXgAAOKBz.jpg)

```
<instructions> 
Input Variable: {argument name="object" default="[INSERT OBJECT]"} (e.g., A Sneaker, A Human Skull, A Cheeseburger, The Letter 'A')

System Instruction:
Reimagine the Input Object as a complex, high-performance Cyber-Industrial Assembly.

1.  Deconstruction:
   The Shell: Replace the object's natural skin with Matte Black Carbon Fiber and Gunmetal Grey Polymer.
   The Segmentation: The object is not solid. It is segmented into distinct panels (like Iron Man armor or a high-end camera body), held together by visible Hex Bolts and Rivets.
   The Gaps: Between the panels, leave small gaps to reveal the internal mechanics.

2.  Internal Mechanics :
   The Piping: Where organic veins or structure would be, insert Bundled Industrial Cabling and Braided Steel Hoses.
   The Flow: These cables must look functional, routing power from a central core to the extremities of the object.
   The Glow (The Soul):
       Color: Identify the "Spirit Color" of the object (e.g., Burger = Amber/Orange; Skull = Cyan/Blue; Sneaker = Neon Green).
       Source: Hidden LED strips and neon tubes run parallel to the cables, casting a strong internal glow that spills out from the panel gaps.

3. The Narrative Micro-Detail (The Greebles):
   Scale Indicators: Embed tiny technical details to sell the scale.
       Vents: Cooling fans or intake grilles.
       Text: Tiny white serial numbers and warning labels (e.g., "CAUTION: HOT", "NO STEP") printed on the casing.
       The "City" (Optional): If the object is large enough, tiny architectural elements (antennas, platforms) can grow out of the mechanical base.

4. Visual Syntax & Composition:
   Background: Clean Studio Grey (Infinite Curve). The focus is entirely on the object's silhouette.
   Lighting:
       Key Light: Soft white studio light to highlight the texture of the carbon fiber weave.
       Rim Light: A sharp backlight to define the edge of the object against the grey background.
       Bloom: The internal colored LEDs must have a soft "Octane Bloom" effect.

5. Render Style:
   Aesthetic: Hard Surface Modeling, "Tech-Wear" Fashion, High-End Automotive Design.
   Camera: Isometric or 3/4 Product Shot angle.

Output: Photorealistic 3D Render, 8k, Highly Detailed Textures (Carbon Fiber, Brushed Metal, Rubber).
</instructions>
```

[[Hard Surface Modeling]]

### 132. 安娜·德·阿玛斯 (Ana de Armas) 和西德尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 的低画质智能手机自拍

### 133. 泼墨风格肖像画

### 141. 新中式美学高端商务肖像

**Author**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: zh

> 一个高度结构化的中文提示，用于生成一张身着红色旗袍的年轻东亚女性高端商业肖像，采用“新中式”美学风格。提示中详细说明了复杂的 Gobo 灯光（投射剪纸艺术阴影）、微距镜头细节以及超写实皮肤纹理（毳毛、次表面散射），以营造出喜庆、高饱和度的视觉效果。

![新中式美学高端商务肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804109829_rmi8ly_G95yDuhWAAAQ6Fk.jpg)
![新中式美学高端商务肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804109944_7m8ajl_G96ElXabUAAKxHh.jpg)

```
1. 宏观风格与媒介
- 核心媒介: 高清商业人像摄影 (High-end Commercial Photography)
- 美学流派: 新中式美学 (New Chinese Style), 节日时尚大片

2. 主体与IP身份
- 核心主体: 年轻东亚女性侧颜特写 (Close-up profile of young Asian woman)
- IP/名人锁定: 穿着{argument name="服装颜色" default="红色"}旗袍 (Red Cheongsam), 佩戴珍珠项链与红色花卉耳环

3. 世界逻辑与物理
- 物理法则: 真实光学投影 (Real optical projection), 面部光影贴合面部起伏
- 空间构成: 人眼平视视角 (Eye-level), 极近距离接触

4. 数据与信息层
- 文本提取: 无文本
- 品牌与符号: {argument name="前景元素" default="红色剪纸艺术前景"} (Red paper-cut art foreground) - 包含仙鹤、蝴蝶与牡丹纹样

5. 材质与纹理
- 核心材质: 超写实皮肤质感 (Hyper-realistic skin), 哑光卡纸 (Matte cardstock), 温润珍珠
- 触感细节: 逆光下可见的面部绒毛 (Visible vellus hair backlit), 次表面散射效果 (Subsurface scattering)

6. 光影与氛围
- 光照模型: Gobo投影布光 (Gobo lighting/Projected shadows) - 复杂的镂空花纹光影投射在人物面部
- 整体氛围: 金色暖阳侧逆光 (Warm golden hour light), 高饱和度喜庆红调, 梦幻且清晰

7. 技术参数
- 镜头与渲染: 85mm-100mm 微距镜头 (Macro lens), 浅景深 (Shallow depth of field), 前景虚化 (Bokeh foreground)
- 构图指令: 框式构图 (Framed composition), --ar 3:4
```

[[Subsurface Scattering]]

---

### 142. Precure 变身设计系统提示

**Author**: [kussie9216](https://x.com/kussie9216)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个针对 Nano Banana Pro 的详细系统提示，它将扮演魔法少女动漫的“首席设计师”，接收一个角色图像输入，并生成一个“光之美少女”变身设计。该提示规定了设计过程的每一步，包括主题选择、方向、颜色、命名约定、发型、服装、眼睛、配饰、姿势以及最终的口号，确保结果符合既定的光之美少女美学。

![Precure 变身设计系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682257635_ohhgup_G958TFFboAARlAW.jpg)

```
# あなたの役割
あなたは女児向けアニメのチーフデザイナーです。
あなたの使命は私の要求に従い女児向けアニメのキャラクターとしてふさわしいキャラクターをデザインすることです。

# あなたへの要求
私が提示したキャラクターがプリキュアに変身した姿をデザインしてください。
**プリキュアシリーズに登場しても違和感のないデザインとしてください。**

# デザインの手順
以下の流れでデザインを進めてください。

## モチーフの決定
私が提示したキャラクターのイメージに合ったモチーフを考案してください。
**キャラクターの特徴を捉え、的確なモチーフを選定してください。**
**入力画像の背景等の要素は加味せず、キャラクターの特徴のみで考えてください。**
モチーフは多彩な候補から選択してください。
例えば以下のようなもの
- 自然(空、大地、海など)
- 動物(犬、猫、うさぎなど)
- 植物(様々な花など)
- 食物(果物など)
- 感情(愛、喜びなど)
- 概念的なもの(平和、高貴など)

## 方向性の決定
デザインするキャラクターの方向性を決定してください。
**キャラクターの特徴を捉え、キャラクターに合った方向性を見出してください**
例えば以下のようなもの
- 可愛らしい
- 美しい
- 勇敢
- コミカル

## イメージカラーの決定
キャラクターのイメージカラーを決定してください。
**キャラクターのイメージ、決定したモチーフにふさわしい色を選択してください。**
色は赤、青、黄、緑、紫など鮮やかな色を基本とし、茶やグレーのような暗い色は避けてください。
ただしキャラクターのイメージに合っていれば黒、白は使用可とします。

## 名前の決定
キャラクターのプリキュアとしての名前を決定してください。
名前はキュア○○("キュア"を除き3～6文字程度が望ましい)とする必要があります。
○○の部分はキャラクターのモチーフを連想させる名前としてください。
(例えばモチーフが星であればスター、エトワール、ステラなど)
基本的に外国語の単語を使用するようにしてください。
語感の柔らかい英語、フランス語、イタリア語等が望ましく、語感の強いドイツ語やロシア語等の使用は
注意する必要があります。
**既存のプリキュアの名前と被らないようにすること**

## キャラクターデザインの決定
**プリキュアとしてふさわしいデザインとする必要があります。**

### 髪
元となるキャラクターの髪色と同系統で明るく鮮やかな色としてください。
例えば以下のような変化
- 赤→ピンク
- 黒→青や緑
- 茶→金髪
髪型は元となるキャラクターの髪型をボリュームアップし大げさにしたようなデザインが基本となります。
ただし元となるキャラクターには無いもの(例としてショートカットのキャラクターに大きなツインテール)を
追加することも可能とします。

### 衣装
モチーフをイメージしたデザインを基本とします。ただしモチーフそのままのデザインは避け、モチーフを
連想させる程度の意匠としてください。
色はキャラクターのイメージカラーをベースとします。
また、キャラクターの方向性も反映させてください。
例えば
- 可愛らしい方向性であればフリル等をあしらった可愛い意匠
- 美しい方向性であれば流線的で上品な意匠
- 勇敢な方向性であれば鋭角で活動的な意匠
- コミカルな方向性であればポップで楽しげな意匠

### 目
目は以下の例のようなデザインにしてください。
- 元のキャラクターより明るく鮮やかな色にする
- 目の中に星やハートを描き加える

### アクセサリー
イヤリング、ティアラ等のアクセサリーをつけてください。

### 持ち物
**プリキュアは徒手空拳で戦うのが基本なので手持ち武器は厳禁とします。**
基本的に何も持たせてはいけません。

## 決めポーズ
**変身ヒロインの決めポーズとしてふさわしい見栄えのするポーズとしてください。**
ポーズのデザイン、ポーズ時の表情はキャラクターの方向性を考慮してください。(可愛らしい、勇敢等)

## 名乗り口上
キャラクターの名乗り口上を考案してください。
モチーフと関連付けた口上としてください。
例として
- 花がモチーフ：「大地に咲く一輪の花」
- 星がモチーフ：「宇宙に輝くキラキラ星」
- 空がモチーフ：「無限に広がる青い空」
**例をそのまま使用しないこと**

# 最終的な成果物
ここまででデザインしたものを1枚のイラストに仕上げてください。
以下の要素は必須とします。
- デザインしたプリキュアが決めポーズを取っている構図とする。
- 背景はイメージカラーを基調としたキラキラ輝く空間とする。またモチーフをあしらってもよい。
- イラストの下部に名乗り口上と名前を書く。
  - 2行に分け、1行目は名乗り口上+「！」、2行目は名前+「！！」とすること。
  - フォントはキャラクターの方向性を反映させること。可愛らしい方向性なら可愛らしい丸文字、勇敢な方向性なら力強い文字など。
```

[[Anime Character Design]]

---

### 152. 狗仔队闪光灯摄影肖像，戴着化装舞会面具

**Author**: [yusra.](https://x.com/chatgptpaglu)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张具有狗仔队美学、高对比度的超写实肖像。它描述了一位身穿银色亮片连衣裙的年轻女子，在夜晚的阳台上手持威尼斯假面舞会面具，强调了强烈的相机闪光灯照明、浓重的阴影，以及亮片和皮肤毛孔等超细节纹理。

### 155. 科学理论可视化生成器

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多阶段提示，旨在将抽象的科学理论或公式（如黑洞）可视化为超现实的、不可能的建筑结构。它始于一个二维的符号媒介（例如，黑板上的粉笔字），然后将线条挤压成一个坚实的三维结构，其中有一个微小的科学家正在观察这个创造物。

![科学理论可视化生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682094478_zeo8ac_G9xfX3gWwAAZm_W.jpg)

```
<instructions> do this for {argument name="scientific concept" default="black holes"}
  Input Variable:   {argument name="theorem or formula" default="[Theorem / Formula]"}
Phase 1: Schematic Decomposition
Analyze the Notation: Identify the primary visual language of the scientist (Chalk on blackboard? Ink on parchment? Pencil on graph paper?).
Identify the "Structure": If this theory were a building, what would it look like?
Logic: Chaos Theory -> Fractal Spire. Thermodynamics -> Engine Block.
Phase 2: The Dimensional Transition
The Base: A flat surface covered in the [Notation Medium] (e.g., a slate blackboard covered in chalk equations).
The Extrusion: The chalk lines physically lift off the surface. They begin as white wireframes, then gain opacity, then gain texture.
The Climax: At the top of the image, the wireframes have fully solidified into a photorealistic, impossible structure representing the theory.
The Observer: A tiny, scale-model figure of the scientist stands on the flat "2D" section, looking up in awe at the massive "3D" structure they have summoned.
Output: High-Angle Isometric, "Architectural Visualization" style, stark contrast between sketchy lines and solid mass.
</instructions>
```

```
Auto mode
```

### 161. 百科全书式 3D 信息图演变图表

**Author**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: ja

![百科全书式 3D 信息图演变图表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682257077_w4ue6x_G95BL8pbUAAH-vn.jpg)

![百科全书式 3D 信息图演变图表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682260897_6f8g30_G95BMw9aUAAHFMq.jpg)

```
役割と主題: 16:9 比率の巨大で百科事典的な 3D インフォグラフィックポスター。タイトル：「THE EVOLUTION OF {argument name="製品名" default="[製品名]"}」。ビジュアルスタイルは、ミュージアム級の製品写真と複雑な技術設計図のハイエンドな融合。

コアラインナップ (年代記): 最初のプロトタイプから最新の未来モデルまで、8〜12の歴史的な {argument name="製品名 2" default="[製品名]"} のバージョンを、完全かつ線形で配置する。それらは、中央を水平に走る測定スケール/定規ベース上に正確に配置される。レンダリング：超リアルな 3D、8K解像度。テクスチャの進化を強調：初期の {argument name="素材の雰囲気" default="[素材の雰囲気]"} の経年劣化と、モダンバージョンの清潔でハイテクな仕上げとの対比を示す。

ブランドの雰囲気 (キャンバス): 背景：深みのある、豊かな [ブランドカラー] のテクスチャード背景。その上に、低不透明度のビンテージ特許図面、手書きのエンジニアリングノート、およびブランドの歴史に関連する新聞の切り抜きの透かしが重層的に配置される。ヘッダー：中央上部に際立った、高コントラストのブランドロゴを配置し、太字のタイポグラフィでタイトルを表示する。

「超高密度」情報レイヤー (パンチスタイル): レイアウトは体系化された情報で圧倒される（「データ美学」の外観を作成する）：
高密度アノテーションネットワーク: 特定の [キーコンポーネント]（例：カーブ、ボタン、エンジン）を、空間に浮かぶコンパクトなテキストブロックやデータテーブルに接続する、数百本の極細の白いヘアライン。
コンテクスチュアルゾーン: 製品の上に浮かぶ「時代モジュール」。図像的なマーカーで異なる歴史的な数十年間を表現する。
拡大インサート: 空きスペースに散在する円形の「ズームイン」レンズ。テクスチャのディテールや内部機構の極端なマクロクローズアップを示す。
技術仕様ストリップ: 最下部に配置された構造化データバー。正確な仕様（重量、寸法、年式、材料コード）をリストアップする。

技術仕様: Octaneレンダー, Unreal Engine 5 の美学, エディトリアルレイアウト, インフォメーションデザインの傑作, ボリュメトリックライティング, シャープフォーカス, プロフェッショナルなカラーグレーディング。--ar 16:9 --v 6.0 --stylize 300 (参考スタイル: コカ・コーラの発展の歴史)
```

![儿童蜡笔画风格生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682112723_va5e1t_G94pNPvbQAA43z0.jpg)

```
Draw {argument name="visual subject" default="[VISUAL]"} as if created by a cheerful 6-year-old on white notebook paper. Use chunky wax-crayon strokes, wobbly outlines, and simple flat shapes. Colors should be bright, bold, and slightly outside the lines, with visible pressure marks and small smudges. Perspective is innocent: objects can float, and size is based on importance, not realism. Faces are dots with curved smiles; hands are mitten blobs; animals are round and friendly. Add playful extras like a sun in a corner, puffy clouds, stars, and hearts. Include uneven scribble shading, a few tiny doodles in the margins, and one or two hand-written labels in childlike spelling.
```

### 179. 地质悬崖突出物符号提示

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多步骤提示公式，用于生成《沙丘》风格的电影级数字绘景。它指示模型将一个字母数字字符或符号转换为瓦迪拉姆（Wadi Rum）式沙漠景观中巨大的地质悬崖突出物（沉积砂岩）。它要求使用特定的比例参考（微小的骆驼和游牧民）和黄金时段的逆光，以营造戏剧性的效果。

```
<instructions> 1. analyze variable: 
Input A is a Single Alphanumeric Character or Symbol (e.g., {argument name="symbol example" default="Sigma"}, Omega, The letter 'Z').
Translate the glyph into a Geological Cliff Protrusion:
Integration: The symbol is NOT a freestanding statue. It must appear to be carved out of, or naturally protruding from, a massive solid rock canyon wall.
Texture: Layered sedimentary sandstone (red rock/orange rock). The horizontal strata lines of the cliff must continue uninterrupted through the symbol, proving it is part of the earth.
Erosion: The edges are soft, chipped, and wind-blasted. No sharp manufacturing lines.

2. The "Immutable" Container (The Vistas):
Goal: A "Wadi Rum" Cinematic Landscape.
The Environment: A vast, open desert floor meeting a towering vertical canyon wall on one side.
The Horizon: The scene opens up to a hazy, infinite desert distance on the opposite side.
Atmosphere: Heavy, warm atmospheric haze (aerial perspective) to separate the foreground rock from the distant hills.

3. The Composition (The Monolith):
Placement: The Symbol (Input A) dominates the left or right third of the frame, physically attached to the rock face, casting a deep shadow against the wall.
Negative Space:* The "holes" in the symbol (e.g., the gap in Sigma) form caves or overhangs that create dramatic pockets of shadow.

4. The Narrative Scale (The Scale Reference):
Mandatory Element: A tiny line of Camels and Bedouin Nomads.
Position: They are walking in a line across the sand at the very bottom of the frame, dwarfed by the cliff.
Ratio: The figures should be microscopic—perhaps 1/100th the height of the symbol—to convey that the cliff is hundreds of feet high.

5. Lighting & Atmosphere:
Lighting:Golden Hour Backlighting. The sun is low on the horizon (in the distance), blasting directly into the camera or hitting the side of the cliff.
Lens Flare: A soft, warm solar flare/bloom is visible where the sun peeks around the rock.
Palette: Monochromatic Deserts. Dusty oranges, beiges, and deep browns.

Output: ONE image, Wide Aspect Ratio (21:9 or 16:9), Cinematic Matte Painting, "Dune" aesthetic, Massive Scale.
</instructions>
```

[[Golden Hour Backlight]]

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的提示，旨在有意地创作出不完美的、具有模拟感的插画，模仿笔记本纸上手绘肖像，并带有红色和黄色钢笔注释，强调富有表现力的线条和逼真的纹理。

```
落書きアートや漫画の注釈（メモ書き）のスタイルを取り入れた、手描きの肖像画イラスト。ノートの紙に、赤と黄色のペンを使って描かれている。被写体の全体を捉えた肖像画で、表情豊かな線描と自然なジェスチャーが特徴。太い輪郭線がまるで光を放っているかのような大胆な表現。周囲には手書きのメモが散りばめられ、ペンのリアルな筆跡や質感が感じられる。4K解像度。
```

### 191. 从种子到货架立体模型流程图提示

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多步骤指令提示，用于使用微缩摄影美学可视化产品（如咖啡或钻石戒指）的生命周期。它要求生成一张图片，图片中包含一个在复古地图上的“从种子到货架”流程图立体模型，其中有三个独特的 3D 小场景（起源、过程、目的地），它们由一条蜿蜒的传送带连接，传送带上装满了产品，所有这些都以 HO 比例（1:87）渲染，并带有移轴效果。

![从种子到货架立体模型流程图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767682202355_t27yr6_G9y3TexW8AAKh1K.jpg)

```
<instruction>
  1. Analyze Input Variable:  
Input A is a Global Commodity with a distinct production lifecycle (e.g., Coffee, Chocolate/Cocoa, Wine, Denim/Cotton).
Deconstruct the lifecycle into   3 Distinct Stages  :
   Stage 1 (The Origin):  The agricultural source (e.g., Coffee Plantation, Cacao Trees).
   Stage 2 (The Process):  The industrial transformation (e.g., Roasting Plant, Fermentation Vats).
   Stage 3 (The Destination):  The retail experience (e.g., A Hipster Cafe, A Chocolatier Shop).
2.  Container (The Map Table):
Goal: A "Seed to Shelf" Flowchart Diorama.
The Base: A large, vintage World Map (blue oceans, pastel continents) laid flat on a wooden dining table.
The Spine: A raised, winding S-Shaped Chute/Conveyor snakes through the center of the image, physically connecting the three stages.
The Flow: The chute is filled with the product, which visually transforms as it moves down the path (e.g., Red Coffee Cherries at the top 
→
→
 Brown Roasted Beans in the middle 
→
→
 Fine Ground Powder at the bottom).
3. The Vignettes (The Stations):
Construct a 3D diorama "Island" at each key point of the S-curve:
Top Station (Origin): A square patch of terrain sitting on the map (e.g., South America). Detailed crops, trees, and farmers harvesting the raw material.
Middle Station (Process): A compact industrial facility sitting on the map (e.g., Europe/USA). Metallic roasters, silos, smoke stacks, and factory workers.
Bottom Station (Destination): An architectural Cutaway Box. The front wall is removed to reveal the interior of a shop (e.g., Espresso machines, tiny customers sitting at tables, baristas serving).
4. The Narrative Scale (The Workers):
Scale: 1:87 (HO Scale) miniature figures.
Action: The figures are not just standing; they are actively moving the product from the "Station" into the "Chute" (e.g., Farmers dumping baskets of cherries into the stream, Factory workers shoveling beans).
5. Lighting & Atmosphere:
Camera Angle: High-Angle Perspective (45-60 degrees). Looking down the length of the table.
Lighting: Natural Daylight. Bright, cheerful, and even. Shadows fall softly on the map.
Depth of Field: Tilt-Shift effect. The top and bottom edges of the table are slightly blurred to make the models look tiny.
Output: ONE image, Vertical Aspect Ratio (4:5), Miniature Photography, Educational Diorama aesthetic.
</instruction>
```

[[Miniature Photography]] [[Tilt-Shift Effect]]

### 193. 科学理论可视化：从 2D 到 3D 挤出

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-04  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多阶段提示，旨在通过从二维符号（黑板上的方程式）过渡到逼真的、不可能的三维建筑结构来可视化抽象的科学理论（如黑洞）。它指定了一个等距高角度视图，并包含一个观察该创造的微小科学家形象。

![科学理论可视化：从 2D 到 3D 挤出](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767606968932_lw6qfd_G9xesymWMAAHgiB.jpg)

```
<instructions> do this for {argument name="scientific concept" default="black holes"}
  Input Variable:   [{argument name="formula type" default="Theorem / Formula"}]
Phase 1: Schematic Decomposition
Analyze the Notation: Identify the primary visual language of the scientist (Chalk on blackboard? Ink on parchment? Pencil on graph paper?).
Identify the "Structure": If this theory were a building, what would it look like?
Logic: Chaos Theory -> Fractal Spire. Thermodynamics -> Engine Block.
Phase 2: The Dimensional Transition
The Base: A flat surface covered in the [Notation Medium] (e.g., a slate blackboard covered in chalk equations).
The Extrusion: The chalk lines physically lift off the surface. They begin as white wireframes, then gain opacity, then gain texture.
The Climax: At the top of the image, the wireframes have fully solidified into a photorealistic, impossible structure representing the theory.
The Observer: A tiny, scale-model figure of the scientist stands on the flat "2D" section, looking up in awe at the massive "3D" structure they have summoned.
Output: High-Angle Isometric, "Architectural Visualization" style, stark contrast between sketchy lines and solid mass.
</instructions>
```

[[Isometric View]]

> 一个结构化的提示，用于生成一个 2x2 网格拼贴画，内容为生活方式时尚照片，使用特定的面部参考（Sadie Sink）。场景是一个户外咖啡馆走道，主体穿着一套黑色运动服，手持一杯绿色冰镇饮料，在所有四个画面中都保持着清新、健康、时尚的夏日美学。

### 199. 电影级侧面人像提示词，带逆光和焦外虚化效果

**Author**: [neto.](https://x.com/nettoqw)  **Date**: 2026-01-04  **Language**: en

> 一个用于 Nano Banana Pro 的 JSON 提示词，旨在创作一张电影感十足、氛围浓厚的年轻东亚女性肖像。该提示词强调了特定的姿势（回眸），通过强烈的背光营造出光晕效果，以及透过模糊的前景元素看到的杂乱、怀旧的室内环境（工作室/书店），以实现梦幻、空灵的意境。

![电影级侧面人像提示词，带逆光和焦外虚化效果](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767607071235_h3omgl_G91kfreXYAAIRKX.jpg)

```
{
  "subject": {
    "description": "Young East Asian woman, positioned in profile turning to look back at the viewer.",
    "pose": "Looking over shoulder, slight head tilt, body angled away from camera.",
    "expression": "Soft, neutral to slightly melancholic, contemplative gaze, lips slightly parted."
  },
  "clothing": {
    "upper_body": "Dark, structured jacket or blazer, possibly pinstriped or textured fabric.",
    "visibility": "Mostly obscured by shadow and foreground elements."
  },
  "hair": {
    "color": "Dark brown to black.",
    "style": "Long, loose, tousled waves, slightly messy texture.",
    "lighting_interaction": "Strongly backlit, creating a glowing halo effect on loose strands (rim lighting)."
  },
  "face": {
    "skin_tone": "Fair/pale with warm undertones.",
    "features": "Soft facial structure, almond-shaped eyes, natural eyebrows.",
    "makeup": "Minimal, 'no-makeup' look, natural lip color."
  },
  "accessories": {
    "visible_items": "None clearly visible due to framing and lighting."
  },
  "environment": {
    "setting": "Cluttered interior space, resembling a workshop, storage room, or old bookstore.",
    "background_elements": "Wooden shelves stacked with indistinct objects, papers, boxes, and plastic packaging.",
    "foreground_elements": "Blurred translucent objects (possibly glass, plastic sheets, or dust covers) creating layers and reflections."
  },
  "lighting": {
    "source": "Natural sunlight streaming through a window on the left.",
    "quality": "Golden hour, warm, diffuse but directional.",
    "effects": "Strong backlighting/rim lighting on hair, volumetric dust motes dancing in the light, lens flares, soft glare, dramatic contrast between light and shadow."
  },
  "camera": {
    "perspective": "Eye-level, shot through a foreground obstruction (glass or clutter).",
    "focus": "Shallow depth of field (bokeh), sharp focus on eyes/face, blurred background and foreground.",
    "lens_character": "Soft focus, film grain simulation, slight bloom effect."
  },
  "style": {
    "aesthetic": "Cinematic, atmospheric, nostalgic, slice-of-life, ethereal.",
    "mood": "Dreamy, intimate, quiet, sentimental.",
    "visual_reference": "Film photography, Japanese photobook style."
  }
}
```

### 200. 奇幻角色设计并排展示表

**Author**: [EJack Yao](https://x.com/yao_ej24569)  **Date**: 2026-01-04  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成并排图像的提示：一个特写面部和一个半身视图，展示的是同一个奇幻角色设计。该角色是一位深色头发、雀斑、拥有迷人蓝眼睛的女性，身穿一件华丽的深蓝色连帽斗篷，上面有金色图案，将优雅与战士的力量融为一体。提示还指定了纯白色背景和边缘照明以增加深度。

![奇幻角色设计并排展示表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767606946928_rua04j_G91h5qkaIAA_VCq.jpg)

```
based on the attached image,
generate a Side by side photo of a close up face, and half body character design (both views are different view of an identical design) of a woman with long, flowing dark hair and a gentle, warm smile. Her face is adorned with delicate freckles, and her striking blue almond-shaped eyes exude kindness. She wears an ornate, deep-blue hooded cloak embellished with intricate gold patterns resembling swirling waves or dragons, evoking a sense of fantasy or ancient nobility. The fabric appears rich and textured, fastened with an elaborate golden clasp at the shoulder. Underneath, glimpses of armored plating suggest a warrior or royal status. The overall aesthetic blends elegance with strength, set against a soft, neutral background that highlights her serene yet powerful presence. close up face on the left, half body on the right, on a flat plain white background, photography with edge lighting for depth, 16:9, 2K
```
